# ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ üîß

OpenClaw ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å **JSON5** ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `~/.openclaw/openclaw.json` (‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î)

‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢ (‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå Pi ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ù‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß + ‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á + ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã `~/.openclaw/workspace`) ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: You usually only need a config to:

- ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (`channels.whatsapp.allowFrom`, `channels.telegram.allowFrom` ‡∏Ø‡∏•‡∏Ø)
- ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏° allowlist ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á (`channels.whatsapp.groups`, `channels.telegram.groups`, `channels.discord.guilds`, `agents.list[].groupChat`)
- ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ã‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° (`messages`)
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (`agents.defaults.workspace` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `agents.list[].workspace`)
- ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ù‡∏±‡∏á (`agents.defaults`) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô (`session`)
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (`agents.list[].identity`)

> **‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤?** ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ [Configuration Examples](/gateway/configuration-examples) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î!

## ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏°‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏î

OpenClaw only accepts configurations that fully match the schema.
OpenClaw ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ Gateway **‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô** ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß:

- Gateway ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏ï
- ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏â‡∏±‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô: `openclaw doctor`, `openclaw logs`, `openclaw health`, `openclaw status`, `openclaw service`, `openclaw help`)
- ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô `openclaw doctor` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î
- ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô `openclaw doctor --fix` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `--yes`) ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢/‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ã‡∏°

Doctor ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏î‡πÜ ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏° `--fix`/`--yes` ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô

## ‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤ + ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏ö‡πâ UI

The Gateway exposes a JSON Schema representation of the config via `config.schema` for UI editors.
Gateway ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ú‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤ JSON ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `config.schema` ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç UI
Control UI ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç **Raw JSON** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏•‡πà

‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏±‡πä‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏ö‡πâ UI ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Æ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏î‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°

‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏ö‡πâ (‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ß) ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≤
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Æ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏î‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å

## ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ + ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï (RPC)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `config.apply` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö + ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï Gateway ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Gateway ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤
It writes a restart sentinel and pings the last active session after the Gateway comes back.

Warning: `config.apply` replaces the **entire config**. If you want to change only a few keys,
use `config.patch` or `openclaw config set`. Keep a backup of `~/.openclaw/openclaw.json`.

Params:

- `raw` (string) ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î JSON5 ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
- `baseHash` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏Æ‡∏ä‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `config.get` (‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)
- `sessionKey` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏Å
- `note` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï
- `restartDelayMs` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô 2000)

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á (‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `gateway call`):

```bash
openclaw gateway call config.get --params '{}' # capture payload.hash
openclaw gateway call config.apply --params '{
  "raw": "{\\n  agents: { defaults: { workspace: \\"~/.openclaw/workspace\\" } }\\n}\\n",
  "baseHash": "<hash-from-config.get>",
  "sessionKey": "agent:main:whatsapp:dm:+15555550123",
  "restartDelayMs": 1000
}'
```

## ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô (RPC)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `config.patch` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ JSON merge patch: It applies JSON merge patch semantics:

- ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏à‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ã‡∏µ‡∏ü
- `null` ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå
- ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà
  ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö `config.apply` ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï Gateway (‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ `sessionKey`)

Params:

- `raw` (string) ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î JSON5 ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô
- `baseHash` (‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô) ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏Æ‡∏ä‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `config.get`
- `sessionKey` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏Å
- `note` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï
- `restartDelayMs` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö) ‚Äî ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô 2000)

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á:

```bash
openclaw gateway call config.get --params '{}' # capture payload.hash
openclaw gateway call config.patch --params '{
  "raw": "{\\n  channels: { telegram: { groups: { \\"*\\": { requireMention: false } } } }\\n}\\n",
  "baseHash": "<hash-from-config.get>",
  "sessionKey": "agent:main:whatsapp:dm:+15555550123",
  "restartDelayMs": 1000
}'
```

## ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥ (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)

```json5
{
  agents: { defaults: { workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace" } },
  channels: { whatsapp: { allowFrom: ["+15555550123"] } },
}
```

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢:

```bash
scripts/sandbox-setup.sh
```

## ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°)

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö @-mentions ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á WhatsApp ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° (‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î):

```json5
{
  agents: {
    defaults: { workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace" },
    list: [
      {
        id: "main",
        groupChat: { mentionPatterns: ["@openclaw", "reisponde"] },
      },
    ],
  },
  channels: {
    whatsapp: {
      // Allowlist is DMs only; including your own number enables self-chat mode.
      allowFrom: ["+15555550123"],
      groups: { "*": { requireMention: true } },
    },
  },
}
```

## ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å (`$include`)

‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á `$include` ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö: This is useful for:

- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå)
- ‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°
- ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô

```json5
// ~/.openclaw/openclaw.json
{
  gateway: { port: 18789 },

  // Include a single file (replaces the key's value)
  agents: { $include: "./agents.json5" },

  // Include multiple files (deep-merged in order)
  broadcast: {
    $include: ["./clients/mueller.json5", "./clients/schmidt.json5"],
  },
}
```

```json5
// ~/.openclaw/agents.json5
{
  defaults: { sandbox: { mode: "all", scope: "session" } },
  list: [{ id: "main", workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace" }],
}
```

### ‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô

- **‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß**: ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡πá‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏à‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ `$include`
- **‡∏≠‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå**: ‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö (‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô)
- **‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á includes (‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≤)
- **‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á + ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå/‡∏û‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ü**: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö (‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πá‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏à‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πå)

```json5
// Sibling keys override included values
{
  $include: "./base.json5", // { a: 1, b: 2 }
  b: 99, // Result: { a: 1, b: 99 }
}
```

### Nested includes

‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á `$include` ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î 10 ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö):

```json5
// clients/mueller.json5
{
  agents: { $include: "./mueller/agents.json5" },
  broadcast: { $include: "./mueller/broadcast.json5" },
}
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á

- **‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå**: ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á
- **‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏
- **‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà**: ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á `../` ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î

```json5
{ "$include": "./sub/config.json5" }      // relative
{ "$include": "/etc/openclaw/base.json5" } // absolute
{ "$include": "../shared/common.json5" }   // parent dir
```

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î

- **‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏¢**: ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
- **‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏™‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î**: ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡πâ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏ß
- **‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥**: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏û‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏é‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå

```json5
// ~/.openclaw/openclaw.json
{
  gateway: { port: 18789, auth: { token: "secret" } },

  // Common agent defaults
  agents: {
    defaults: {
      sandbox: { mode: "all", scope: "session" },
    },
    // Merge agent lists from all clients
    list: { $include: ["./clients/mueller/agents.json5", "./clients/schmidt/agents.json5"] },
  },

  // Merge broadcast configs
  broadcast: {
    $include: ["./clients/mueller/broadcast.json5", "./clients/schmidt/broadcast.json5"],
  },

  channels: { whatsapp: { groupPolicy: "allowlist" } },
}
```

```json5
// ~/.openclaw/clients/mueller/agents.json5
[
  { id: "mueller-transcribe", workspace: "~/clients/mueller/transcribe" },
  { id: "mueller-docs", workspace: "~/clients/mueller/docs" },
]
```

```json5
// ~/.openclaw/clients/mueller/broadcast.json5
{
  "120363403215116621@g.us": ["mueller-transcribe", "mueller-docs"],
}
```

## ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢

### Env vars + `.env`

OpenClaw ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏•‡∏•‡πå launchd/systemd CI ‡∏Ø‡∏•‡∏Ø)

‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î:

- `.env` ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ)
- ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ fallback ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á `.env` ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `~/.openclaw/.env` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `$OPENCLAW_STATE_DIR/.env`)

‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.env` ‡πÉ‡∏î‡πÜ ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà

You can also provide inline env vars in config. These are only applied if the
process env is missing the key (same non-overriding rule):

```json5
{
  env: {
    OPENROUTER_API_KEY: "sk-or-...",
    vars: {
      GROQ_API_KEY: "gsk-...",
    },
  },
}
```

‡∏î‡∏π [/environment](/help/environment) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô

### `env.shellEnv` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö)

‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏ß‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ: ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏î‡πÜ
OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏•‡∏•‡πå‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏î (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö)
‡∏ã‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ source ‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏•‡∏•‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì
This effectively sources your shell profile.

```json5
{
  env: {
    shellEnv: {
      enabled: true,
      timeoutMs: 15000,
    },
  },
}
```

Env var equivalent:

- `OPENCLAW_LOAD_SHELL_ENV=1`
- `OPENCLAW_SHELL_ENV_TIMEOUT_MS=15000`

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πàenv var‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å

‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
`${VAR_NAME}` ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Variables are substituted at config load time, before validation.

```json5
{
  models: {
    providers: {
      "vercel-gateway": {
        apiKey: "${VERCEL_GATEWAY_API_KEY}",
      },
    },
  },
  gateway: {
    auth: {
      token: "${OPENCLAW_GATEWAY_TOKEN}",
    },
  },
}
```

**‡∏Å‡∏é:**

- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà: `[A-Z_][A-Z0-9_]*`
- Missing or empty env vars throw an error at config load
- ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏õ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ `$${VAR}` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå `${VAR}` ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏•‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏±‡∏•
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö `$include` (‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢)

**‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå:**

```json5
{
  models: {
    providers: {
      custom: {
        baseUrl: "${CUSTOM_API_BASE}/v1", // ‚Üí "https://api.example.com/v1"
      },
    },
  },
}
```

### ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô (OAuth + ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πåAPI)

OpenClaw ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô **‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå** (OAuth + ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πåAPI) ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:

- `<agentDir>/auth-profiles.json` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `~/.openclaw/agents/<agentId>/agent/auth-profiles.json`)

‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°: [/concepts/oauth](/concepts/oauth)

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ OAuth ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°:

- `~/.openclaw/credentials/oauth.json` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `$OPENCLAW_STATE_DIR/credentials/oauth.json`)

‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå Pi ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ù‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà:

- `<agentDir>/auth.json` (‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥; ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á)

‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏° (‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå):

- `~/.openclaw/agent/*` (‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ `openclaw doctor` ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á `~/.openclaw/agents/<defaultAgentId>/agent/*`)

Overrides:

- ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ OAuth (‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô): `OPENCLAW_OAUTH_DIR`
- ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô): `OPENCLAW_AGENT_DIR` (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥), `PI_CODING_AGENT_DIR` (‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°)

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ `oauth.json` ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á `auth-profiles.json`

### `auth`

Optional metadata for auth profiles. ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏°‡∏õ‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ + ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö failover

```json5
{
  auth: {
    profiles: {
      "anthropic:me@example.com": { provider: "anthropic", mode: "oauth", email: "me@example.com" },
      "anthropic:work": { provider: "anthropic", mode: "api_key" },
    },
    order: {
      anthropic: ["anthropic:me@example.com", "anthropic:work"],
    },
  },
}
```

### `agents.list[].identity`

‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ UX
‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢ onboarding ‡∏ö‡∏ô macOS This is written by the macOS onboarding assistant.

‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á):

- `messages.ackReaction` ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `identity.emoji` ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á **‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà** (‡∏ñ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô üëÄ)
- `agents.list[].groupChat.mentionPatterns` ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `identity.name`/`identity.emoji` ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ ‚Äú@Samantha‚Äù ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Telegram/Slack/Discord/Google Chat/iMessage/WhatsApp)
- `identity.avatar` ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ URL ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏Å‡∏•/data URL ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÇ‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏•‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå Local files must live inside the agent workspace.

`identity.avatar` ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö:

- ‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ò‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå)
- URL `http(s)`
- URI `data:`

```json5
{
  agents: {
    list: [
      {
        id: "main",
        identity: {
          name: "Samantha",
          theme: "helpful sloth",
          emoji: "ü¶•",
          avatar: "avatars/samantha.png",
        },
      },
    ],
  },
}
```

### `wizard`

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ã‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏î CLI (`onboard`, `configure`, `doctor`)

```json5
{
  wizard: {
    lastRunAt: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
    lastRunVersion: "2026.1.4",
    lastRunCommit: "abc1234",
    lastRunCommand: "configure",
    lastRunMode: "local",
  },
}
```

### `logging`

- ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `/tmp/openclaw/openclaw-YYYY-MM-DD.log`
- ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ò‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á `logging.file` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô `/tmp/openclaw/openclaw.log`
- ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πå‡∏û‡∏∏‡∏ï‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏ã‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô:
  - `logging.consoleLevel` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô `info` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô `debug` ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `--verbose`)
  - `logging.consoleStyle` (`pretty` | `compact` | `json`)
- ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö:
  - `logging.redactSensitive` (`off` | `tools`, ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `tools`)
  - `logging.redactPatterns` (‡∏≠‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå regex; ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)

```json5
{
  logging: {
    level: "info",
    file: "/tmp/openclaw/openclaw.log",
    consoleLevel: "info",
    consoleStyle: "pretty",
    redactSensitive: "tools",
    redactPatterns: [
      // Example: override defaults with your own rules.
      "\\bTOKEN\\b\\s*[=:]\\s*([\"']?)([^\\s\"']+)\\1",
      "/\\bsk-[A-Za-z0-9_-]{8,}\\b/gi",
    ],
  },
}
```

### `channels.whatsapp.dmPolicy`

‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á (DMs) ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á WhatsApp:

- `"pairing"` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô): ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà; ‡πÄ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
- `"allowlist"`: ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô `channels.whatsapp.allowFrom` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô allow ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)
- `"open"`: ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï DMs ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (**‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ** `channels.whatsapp.allowFrom` ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° `"*"`)
- `"disabled"`: ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏¢ DMs ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î

Pairing codes expire after 1 hour; the bot only sends a pairing code when a new request is created. ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÉ‡∏ô 1 ‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏á ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà DM ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î **3 ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á** ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà:

- `openclaw pairing list whatsapp`
- `openclaw pairing approve whatsapp <code>`

### `channels.whatsapp.allowFrom`

Allowlist ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå E.164 ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á WhatsApp (**‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ DMs**)
‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ `channels.whatsapp.dmPolicy="pairing"` ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà
‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `channels.whatsapp.groupPolicy` + `channels.whatsapp.groupAllowFrom`
If empty and `channels.whatsapp.dmPolicy="pairing"`, unknown senders will receive a pairing code.
For groups, use `channels.whatsapp.groupPolicy` + `channels.whatsapp.groupAllowFrom`.

```json5
{
  channels: {
    whatsapp: {
      dmPolicy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
      allowFrom: ["+15555550123", "+447700900123"],
      textChunkLimit: 4000, // optional outbound chunk size (chars)
      chunkMode: "length", // optional chunking mode (length | newline)
      mediaMaxMb: 50, // optional inbound media cap (MB)
    },
  },
}
```

### `channels.whatsapp.sendReadReceipts`

‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° WhatsApp ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà (‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πä‡∏Å‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô)
‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `true` Default: `true`.

‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ: `channels.whatsapp.accounts.<id>.sendReadReceipts`

```json5
{
  channels: {
    whatsapp: { sendReadReceipts: false },
  },
}
```

### `channels.whatsapp.accounts` (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ)

‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ WhatsApp ‡πÉ‡∏ô Gateway ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß:

```json5
{
  channels: {
    whatsapp: {
      accounts: {
        default: {}, // optional; keeps the default id stable
        personal: {},
        biz: {
          // Optional override. Default: ~/.openclaw/credentials/whatsapp/biz
          // authDir: "~/.openclaw/credentials/whatsapp/biz",
        },
      },
    },
  },
}
```

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ `default` ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏â‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö
- ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô Baileys ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ `openclaw doctor` ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á `whatsapp/default`

### `channels.telegram.accounts` / `channels.discord.accounts` / `channels.googlechat.accounts` / `channels.slack.accounts` / `channels.mattermost.accounts` / `channels.signal.accounts` / `channels.imessage.accounts`

‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á (‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏µ `accountId` ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ `name` ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö):

```json5
{
  channels: {
    telegram: {
      accounts: {
        default: {
          name: "Primary bot",
          botToken: "123456:ABC...",
        },
        alerts: {
          name: "Alerts bot",
          botToken: "987654:XYZ...",
        },
      },
    },
  },
}
```

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `default` ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ `accountId` (CLI + ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á)
- ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô env ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ **‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô** ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô (‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á ‡∏Ø‡∏•‡∏Ø) ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ apply to all accounts unless overridden per account.
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `bindings[].match.accountId` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á agents.defaults ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° (`agents.list[].groupChat` + `messages.groupChat`)

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô **‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á** (‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ô regex)
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° WhatsApp, Telegram, Discord, Google Chat ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ iMessage Applies to WhatsApp, Telegram, Discord, Google Chat, and iMessage group chats.

**‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á:**

- **Metadata mentions**: Native platform @-mentions (e.g., WhatsApp tap-to-mention). **‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≤**: @-mentions ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏° (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô WhatsApp) ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á WhatsApp (‡∏î‡∏π `channels.whatsapp.allowFrom`)
- **‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°**: regex ‡πÉ‡∏ô `agents.list[].groupChat.mentionPatterns` ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á Always checked regardless of self-chat mode.
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á `mentionPattern`)

```json5
{
  messages: {
    groupChat: { historyLimit: 50 },
  },
  agents: {
    list: [{ id: "main", groupChat: { mentionPatterns: ["@openclaw", "openclaw"] } }],
  },
}
```

`messages.groupChat.historyLimit` ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ `channels.<channel> Channels can override with `channels.<channel>.historyLimit`(‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠`channels.<channel>.accounts.\*.historyLimit`‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ) ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á`0`‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ Set`0\` to disable history wrapping.

#### ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ DM

DM conversations use session-based history managed by the agent. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤ DM ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô DM:

```json5
{
  channels: {
    telegram: {
      dmHistoryLimit: 30, // limit DM sessions to 30 user turns
      dms: {
        "123456789": { historyLimit: 50 }, // per-user override (user ID)
      },
    },
  },
}
```

‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤:

1. ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ DM: `channels.<provider>.dms[userId].historyLimit`
2. ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£: `channels.<provider>.dmHistoryLimit`
3. ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î (‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î)

‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö: `telegram`, `whatsapp`, `discord`, `slack`, `signal`, `imessage`, `msteams`

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ `[]`):

```json5
{
  agents: {
    list: [
      { id: "work", groupChat: { mentionPatterns: ["@workbot", "\\+15555550123"] } },
      { id: "personal", groupChat: { mentionPatterns: ["@homebot", "\\+15555550999"] } },
    ],
  },
}
```

Mention gating defaults live per channel (`channels.whatsapp.groups`, `channels.telegram.groups`, `channels.imessage.groups`, `channels.discord.guilds`). ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á (`channels.whatsapp.groups`, `channels.telegram.groups`, `channels.imessage.groups`, `channels.discord.guilds`) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î `*.groups` ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô allowlist ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° `"*"` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö **‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞** ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à @-mentions):

```json5
{
  channels: {
    whatsapp: {
      // Include your own number to enable self-chat mode (ignore native @-mentions).
      allowFrom: ["+15555550123"],
      groups: { "*": { requireMention: true } },
    },
  },
  agents: {
    list: [
      {
        id: "main",
        groupChat: {
          // Only these text patterns will trigger responses
          mentionPatterns: ["reisponde", "@openclaw"],
        },
      },
    ],
  },
}
```

### ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° (‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `channels.*.groupPolicy` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°/‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà:

```json5
{
  channels: {
    whatsapp: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      groupAllowFrom: ["+15551234567"],
    },
    telegram: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      groupAllowFrom: ["tg:123456789", "@alice"],
    },
    signal: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      groupAllowFrom: ["+15551234567"],
    },
    imessage: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      groupAllowFrom: ["chat_id:123"],
    },
    msteams: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      groupAllowFrom: ["user@org.com"],
    },
    discord: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      guilds: {
        GUILD_ID: {
          channels: { help: { allow: true } },
        },
      },
    },
    slack: {
      groupPolicy: "allowlist",
      channels: { "#general": { allow: true } },
    },
  },
}
```

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- `"open"`: ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° allowlist; ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á
- `"disabled"`: ‡∏ö‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°/‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
- `"allowlist"`: ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°/‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á allowlist
- `channels.defaults.groupPolicy` ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `groupPolicy` ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á
- WhatsApp/Telegram/Signal/iMessage/Microsoft Teams ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `groupAllowFrom` (fallback: `allowFrom`)
- Discord/Slack ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ allowlist ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á (`channels.discord.guilds.*.channels`, `channels.slack.channels`)
- Group DMs (Discord/Slack) ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ `dm.groupEnabled` + `dm.groupChannels`
- ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ `groupPolicy: "allowlist"` (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ `channels.defaults.groupPolicy`) ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ allowlist ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ö‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å

### ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (`agents.list` + `bindings`)

‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã, `agentDir`, ‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å)
‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô Gateway ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å
Inbound messages are routed to an agent via bindings.

- `agents.list[]`: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå
  - `id`: id ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà (‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô)
  - `default`: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö; ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å
    If none are set, the **first entry** in the list is the default agent.
  - `name`: ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå
  - `workspace`: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô `~/.openclaw/workspace-<agentId>` (‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö `main` ‡∏ñ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö `agents.defaults.workspace`)
  - `agentDir`: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô `~/.openclaw/agents/<agentId>/agent`
  - `model`: ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà `agents.defaults.model`
    - ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á: `"provider/model"` ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ `agents.defaults.model.primary`
    - ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡πá‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏à‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πå: `{ primary, fallbacks }` (fallback ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà `agents.defaults.model.fallbacks`; `[]` ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î fallback ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ)
  - `identity`: ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠/‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏°/‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏à‡∏¥‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏û‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á + ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô ack)
  - `groupChat`: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (`mentionPatterns`)
  - `sandbox`: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å sandbox ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà `agents.defaults.sandbox`)
    - `mode`: `"off"` | `"non-main"` | `"all"`
    - `workspaceAccess`: `"none"` | `"ro"` | `"rw"`
    - `scope`: `"session"` | `"agent"` | `"shared"`
    - `workspaceRoot`: ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã sandbox ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
    - `docker`: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà docker ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `image`, `network`, `env`, `setupCommand`, limits; ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `scope: "shared"`)
    - `browser`: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå sandbox ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `scope: "shared"`)
    - `prune`: ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏á sandbox ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `scope: "shared"`)
  - `subagents`: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô sub-agent ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå
    - `allowAgents`: allowlist id ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö `sessions_spawn` ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ (`["*"]` = ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πÉ‡∏î‡πÜ ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)
  - `tools`: ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á sandbox)
    - `profile`: ‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô
    - `allow`: ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï
    - `deny`: ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° (‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏∞)
- `agents.defaults`: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏£‡πå
- `bindings[]`: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á `agentId`
  - `match.channel` (‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô)
  - `match.accountId` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö; `*` = ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏î‡∏Å‡πá‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ)
  - `match.peer` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö; `{ kind: dm|group|channel, id }`)
  - `match.guildId` / `match.teamId` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö; ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á)

‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô:

1. `match.peer`
2. `match.guildId`
3. `match.teamId`
4. `match.accountId`
5. `match.accountId: "*"`
6. ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô (`agents.list[].default` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `"main"`)

‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ä‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô `bindings` ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ä‡∏ô‡∏∞

#### ‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå)

‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏°‡∏µ sandbox + ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Gateway ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß: Use this to mix access
levels in one gateway:

- **‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö** (‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß)
- ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ **‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß** + ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã
- **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö** (‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°/‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô)

‡∏î‡∏π [Multi-Agent Sandbox & Tools](/tools/multi-agent-sandbox-tools)

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏° (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ sandbox):

```json5
{
  agents: {
    list: [
      {
        id: "personal",
        workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace-personal",
        sandbox: { mode: "off" },
      },
    ],
  },
}
```

‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß + ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß:

```json5
{
  agents: {
    list: [
      {
        id: "family",
        workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace-family",
        sandbox: {
          mode: "all",
          scope: "agent",
          workspaceAccess: "ro",
        },
        tools: {
          allow: [
            "read",
            "sessions_list",
            "sessions_history",
            "sessions_send",
            "sessions_spawn",
            "session_status",
          ],
          deny: ["write", "edit", "apply_patch", "exec", "process", "browser"],
        },
      },
    ],
  },
}
```

‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö (‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°/‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô):

```json5
{
  agents: {
    list: [
      {
        id: "public",
        workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace-public",
        sandbox: {
          mode: "all",
          scope: "agent",
          workspaceAccess: "none",
        },
        tools: {
          allow: [
            "sessions_list",
            "sessions_history",
            "sessions_send",
            "sessions_spawn",
            "session_status",
            "whatsapp",
            "telegram",
            "slack",
            "discord",
            "gateway",
          ],
          deny: [
            "read",
            "write",
            "edit",
            "apply_patch",
            "exec",
            "process",
            "browser",
            "canvas",
            "nodes",
            "cron",
            "gateway",
            "image",
          ],
        },
      },
    ],
  },
}
```

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á: ‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ WhatsApp ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå:

```json5
{
  agents: {
    list: [
      { id: "home", default: true, workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace-home" },
      { id: "work", workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace-work" },
    ],
  },
  bindings: [
    { agentId: "home", match: { channel: "whatsapp", accountId: "personal" } },
    { agentId: "work", match: { channel: "whatsapp", accountId: "biz" } },
  ],
  channels: {
    whatsapp: {
      accounts: {
        personal: {},
        biz: {},
      },
    },
  },
}
```

### `tools.agentToAgent` (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö)

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:

```json5
{
  tools: {
    agentToAgent: {
      enabled: false,
      allow: ["home", "work"],
    },
  },
}
```

### `messages.queue`

‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

```json5
{
  messages: {
    queue: {
      mode: "collect", // steer | followup | collect | steer-backlog (steer+backlog ok) | interrupt (queue=steer legacy)
      debounceMs: 1000,
      cap: 20,
      drop: "summarize", // old | new | summarize
      byChannel: {
        whatsapp: "collect",
        telegram: "collect",
        discord: "collect",
        imessage: "collect",
        webchat: "collect",
      },
    },
  },
}
```

### `messages.inbound`

‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å **‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏ï‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á + ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏î/ID ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö Debouncing is scoped per channel + conversation
and uses the most recent message for reply threading/IDs.

```json5
{
  messages: {
    inbound: {
      debounceMs: 2000, // 0 disables
      byChannel: {
        whatsapp: 5000,
        slack: 1500,
        discord: 1500,
      },
    },
  },
}
```

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° **‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô**; ‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠/‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ü‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ä‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
- ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏° (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `/queue`, `/new`) ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á

### `commands` (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï)

‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πá‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå

```json5
{
  commands: {
    native: "auto", // register native commands when supported (auto)
    text: true, // parse slash commands in chat messages
    bash: false, // allow ! (alias: /bash) (host-only; requires tools.elevated allowlists)
    bashForegroundMs: 2000, // bash foreground window (0 backgrounds immediately)
    config: false, // allow /config (writes to disk)
    debug: false, // allow /debug (runtime-only overrides)
    restart: false, // allow /restart + gateway restart tool
    useAccessGroups: true, // enforce access-group allowlists/policies for commands
  },
}
```

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° **‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß** ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ã‡πå‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ `/`
- `commands.text: false` ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏£‡πå‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï
- `commands.native: "auto"` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô) ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ü‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Discord/Telegram ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Slack
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á `commands.native: true|false` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ `channels.discord.commands.native`, `channels.telegram.commands.native`, `channels.slack.commands.native` `false` ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏ô Discord/Telegram ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°
- `channels.telegram.customCommands` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏π‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï Telegram ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏° 2. ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô; ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ü‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô
- `commands.bash: true` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `! 3. <cmd>` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏•‡∏•‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Æ‡∏™‡∏ï‡πå (`/bash <cmd>` ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ù‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô) <cmd>`‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏•‡∏•‡πå‡πÇ‡∏Æ‡∏™‡∏ï‡πå ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ`tools.elevated.enabled`‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ allowlist ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô`tools.elevated.allowFrom.<channel>\`
- `commands.bashForegroundMs` ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á bash 4. ‡∏Ç‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô bash ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏≠ `! 5. <cmd>` ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò (‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô) <cmd>\` requests are rejected (one at a time).
- `commands.config: true` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `/config`
- 7. .configWrites`‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: true)8. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö`/config set|unset`‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ID ‡∏ã‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡πä‡∏õ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Telegram, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ID ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Slack) 9. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å
       allowlist/‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á`commands.useAccessGroups\`
- `commands.debug: true` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `/debug`
- `commands.restart: true` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `/restart`
- `commands.useAccessGroups: false` ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° allowlist/‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°
- ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏ä‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏ü‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ **‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï** 10. WhatsApp ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πå (Baileys Web)

### `web` (‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πå‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö WhatsApp)

11. ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà 12. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `web.enabled: false` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô
12. OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Telegram ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å `channels.telegram` ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà

```json5
{
  web: {
    enabled: true,
    heartbeatSeconds: 60,
    reconnect: {
      initialMs: 2000,
      maxMs: 120000,
      factor: 1.4,
      jitter: 0.2,
      maxAttempts: 0,
    },
  },
}
```

### `channels.telegram` (‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï)

14. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `channels.telegram.enabled: false` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Telegram ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å `channels.telegram`
    ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `channels.telegram.botToken` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `channels.telegram.tokenFile`) ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏µ `TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô fallback
    ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á `channels.telegram.enabled: false` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
15. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `channels.telegram.accounts` (‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô)
16. ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô 17. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `channels.telegram.configWrites: false` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Telegram (‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ ID ‡∏ã‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡πä‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ `/config set|unset`)
17. ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á:

```json5
{
  channels: {
    telegram: {
      enabled: true,
      botToken: "your-bot-token",
      dmPolicy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
      allowFrom: ["tg:123456789"], // optional; "open" requires ["*"]
      groups: {
        "*": { requireMention: true },
        "-1001234567890": {
          allowFrom: ["@admin"],
          systemPrompt: "Keep answers brief.",
          topics: {
            "99": {
              requireMention: false,
              skills: ["search"],
              systemPrompt: "Stay on topic.",
            },
          },
        },
      },
      customCommands: [
        { command: "backup", description: "Git backup" },
        { command: "generate", description: "Create an image" },
      ],
      historyLimit: 50, // include last N group messages as context (0 disables)
      replyToMode: "first", // off | first | all
      linkPreview: true, // toggle outbound link previews
      streamMode: "partial", // off | partial | block (draft streaming; separate from block streaming)
      draftChunk: {
        // optional; only for streamMode=block
        minChars: 200,
        maxChars: 800,
        breakPreference: "paragraph", // paragraph | newline | sentence
      },
      actions: { reactions: true, sendMessage: true }, // tool action gates (false disables)
      reactionNotifications: "own", // off | own | all
      mediaMaxMb: 5,
      retry: {
        // outbound retry policy
        attempts: 3,
        minDelayMs: 400,
        maxDelayMs: 30000,
        jitter: 0.1,
      },
      network: {
        // transport overrides
        autoSelectFamily: false,
      },
      proxy: "socks5://localhost:9050",
      webhookUrl: "https://example.com/telegram-webhook", // requires webhookSecret
      webhookSecret: "secret",
      webhookPath: "/telegram-webhook",
    },
  },
}
```

19. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Telegram `sendMessageDraft` (‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)

- 20. ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß** (message_thread_id ‡πÉ‡∏ô DM; ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)
- 21. `/reasoning stream` ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢
- 22. ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô [Retry policy](/concepts/retry)
  23. `channels.discord` (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó)

### 24. ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó Discord ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏° (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ):&#xA;‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `channels.discord.accounts` (‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô)

25. ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô 26. {
    channels: {
    discord: {
    enabled: true,
    token: "your-bot-token",
    mediaMaxMb: 8, // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤
    allowBots: false, // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó
    actions: {
    // ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ (false ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î)
    reactions: true,
    stickers: true,
    polls: true,
    permissions: true,
    messages: true,
    threads: true,
    pins: true,
    search: true,
    memberInfo: true,
    roleInfo: true,
    roles: false,
    channelInfo: true,
    voiceStatus: true,
    events: true,
    moderation: false,
    },
    replyToMode: "off", // off | first | all
    dm: {
    enabled: true, // ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î DM ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô false
    policy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
    allowFrom: ["1234567890", "steipete"], // allowlist DM ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å ("open" ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ ["\*"])
    groupEnabled: false, // ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô DM ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°
    groupChannels: ["openclaw-dm"], // allowlist DM ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å
    },
    guilds: {
    "123456789012345678": {
    // guild id (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ slug
    slug: "friends-of-openclaw",
    requireMention: false, // ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå
    reactionNotifications: "own", // off | own | all | allowlist
    users: ["987654321098765432"], // allowlist ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå (‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å)
    channels: {
    general: { allow: true },
    help: {
    allow: true,
    requireMention: true,
    users: ["987654321098765432"],
    skills: ["docs"],
    systemPrompt: "Short answers only.",
    },
    },
    },
    },
    historyLimit: 20, // ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î N ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó
    textChunkLimit: 2000, // ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å (‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£)
    chunkMode: "length", // ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å (length | newline)
    maxLinesPerMessage: 17, // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô UI Discord)
    retry: {
    // ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å
    attempts: 3,
    minDelayMs: 500,
    maxDelayMs: 30000,
    jitter: 0.1,
    },
    },
    },
    }

```json5
27. OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Discord ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å `channels.discord` ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà
```

28. ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `channels.discord.token` ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏µ `DISCORD_BOT_TOKEN` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ fallback ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà `channels.discord.enabled` ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô `false`) 29. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `user:<id>` (DM) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `channel:<id>` (‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á cron/CLI; ID ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò 30. slug ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ `-`; ‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô slug (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ `#` ‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤)
29. ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ guild id ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ 32. ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô
30. ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ `channels.discord.allowBots` (‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á) 34. ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô:
31. ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° `channels.discord.textChunkLimit` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô 2000)

- `off`: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô
- `own`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)
- `all`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
- `allowlist`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `guilds.<id>.users` ‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° (‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô)
  36. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `channels.discord.chunkMode="newline"` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á (‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏ï‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤) ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß 37. ‡πÑ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå Discord ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å ‡∏î‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô `channels.discord.maxLinesPerMessage` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô 17) ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ 2000 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ 38. ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô [Retry policy](/concepts/retry)
  39. `channels.googlechat` (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Æ‡∏∏‡∏Ñ Chat API)

### 40. Google Chat ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Æ‡∏∏‡∏Ñ HTTP ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ (service account)

41. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `channels.googlechat.accounts` (‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô)
42. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô 43. {
    channels: {
    googlechat: {
    enabled: true,
    serviceAccountFile: "/path/to/service-account.json",
    audienceType: "app-url", // app-url | project-number
    audience: "https://gateway.example.com/googlechat",
    webhookPath: "/googlechat",
    botUser: "users/1234567890", // ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å; ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á
    dm: {
    enabled: true,
    policy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
    allowFrom: ["users/1234567890"], // ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å; "open" ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ ["\*"]
    },
    groupPolicy: "allowlist",
    groups: {
    "spaces/AAAA": { allow: true, requireMention: true },
    },
    actions: { reactions: true },
    typingIndicator: "message",
    mediaMaxMb: 20,
    },
    },
    }

```json5
44. JSON ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Service account ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå (`serviceAccount`) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå (`serviceAccountFile`)
```

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- 45. ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ fallback ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `GOOGLE_CHAT_SERVICE_ACCOUNT` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `GOOGLE_CHAT_SERVICE_ACCOUNT_FILE`
- 46. `audienceType` + `audience` ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Æ‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ Chat
- 47. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `spaces/<spaceId>` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `users/<userId|email>` ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á
- 48. `channels.slack` (‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ã‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ï)

### 49. Slack ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î Socket ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ:

50. {
    channels: {
    slack: {
    enabled: true,
    botToken: "xoxb-...",
    appToken: "xapp-...",
    dm: {
    enabled: true,
    policy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
    allowFrom: ["U123", "U456", "_"], // ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å; "open" ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ ["_"]
    groupEnabled: false,
    groupChannels: ["G123"],
    },
    channels: {
    C123: { allow: true, requireMention: true, allowBots: false },
    "#general": {
    allow: true,
    requireMention: true,
    allowBots: false,
    users: ["U123"],
    skills: ["docs"],
    systemPrompt: "Short answers only.",
    },
    },
    historyLimit: 50, // ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á/‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î N ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó (0 ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î)
    allowBots: false,
    reactionNotifications: "own", // off | own | all | allowlist
    reactionAllowlist: ["U123"],
    replyToMode: "off", // off | first | all
    thread: {
    historyScope: "thread", // thread | channel
    inheritParent: false,
    },
    actions: {
    reactions: true,
    messages: true,
    pins: true,
    memberInfo: true,
    emojiList: true,
    },
    slashCommand: {
    enabled: true,
    name: "openclaw",
    sessionPrefix: "slack:slash",
    ephemeral: true,
    },
    textChunkLimit: 4000,
    chunkMode: "length",
    mediaMaxMb: 20,
    },
    },
    }

```json5
{
  channels: {
    slack: {
      enabled: true,
      botToken: "xoxb-...",
      appToken: "xapp-...",
      dm: {
        enabled: true,
        policy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
        allowFrom: ["U123", "U456", "*"], // optional; "open" requires ["*"]
        groupEnabled: false,
        groupChannels: ["G123"],
      },
      channels: {
        C123: { allow: true, requireMention: true, allowBots: false },
        "#general": {
          allow: true,
          requireMention: true,
          allowBots: false,
          users: ["U123"],
          skills: ["docs"],
          systemPrompt: "Short answers only.",
        },
      },
      historyLimit: 50, // include last N channel/group messages as context (0 disables)
      allowBots: false,
      reactionNotifications: "own", // off | own | all | allowlist
      reactionAllowlist: ["U123"],
      replyToMode: "off", // off | first | all
      thread: {
        historyScope: "thread", // thread | channel
        inheritParent: false,
      },
      actions: {
        reactions: true,
        messages: true,
        pins: true,
        memberInfo: true,
        emojiList: true,
      },
      slashCommand: {
        enabled: true,
        name: "openclaw",
        sessionPrefix: "slack:slash",
        ephemeral: true,
      },
      textChunkLimit: 4000,
      chunkMode: "length",
      mediaMaxMb: 20,
    },
  },
}
```

1. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `channels.slack.accounts` (‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô multi-account ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô) 2. ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° (Env) ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô

3. OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Slack ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß (‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `SLACK_BOT_TOKEN` + `SLACK_APP_TOKEN`) 4. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `user:<id>` (DM) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `channel:<id>` ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á cron/CLI
4. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `channels.slack.configWrites: false` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Slack (‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ channel ID ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ `/config set|unset`)

6. ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô 7. ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ `channels.slack.allowBots` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `channels.slack.channels.<id>.allowBots`

8. ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô:

- `off`: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô
- `own`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)
- `all`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
- 9. `allowlist`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `channels.slack.reactionAllowlist` ‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô)

10. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏î:

- 11. `channels.slack.thread.historyScope` ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏î‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏î (`thread`, ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏• (`channel`)
- 12. `channels.slack.thread.inheritParent` ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏∑‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏õ‡∏ï‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: false)

13. ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Slack (‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î/‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠ `slack`):

| Action group | Default | Notes                                                 |
| ------------ | ------- | ----------------------------------------------------- |
| reactions    | enabled | 14. React + ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô |
| messages     | enabled | ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô/‡∏™‡πà‡∏á/‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç/‡∏•‡∏ö                                     |
| pins         | enabled | ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏î/‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å/‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£                             |
| memberInfo   | enabled | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å                                          |
| emojiList    | enabled | ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏à‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á                               |

### 15. `channels.mattermost` (‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó)

Mattermost ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏±‡πä‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
16. ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô: `openclaw plugins install @openclaw/mattermost` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `./extensions/mattermost` ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å git checkout)

17. Mattermost ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö base URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ü‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì:

```json5
18. {
  channels: {
    mattermost: {
      enabled: true,
      botToken: "mm-token",
      baseUrl: "https://chat.example.com",
      dmPolicy: "pairing",
      chatmode: "oncall", // oncall | onmessage | onchar
      oncharPrefixes: [">", "!"],
      textChunkLimit: 4000,
      chunkMode: "length",
    },
  },
}
```

19. OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Mattermost ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ (‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ó + base URL) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß 20. ‡πÇ‡∏ó‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô + base URL ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `channels.mattermost.botToken` + `channels.mattermost.baseUrl` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `MATTERMOST_BOT_TOKEN` + `MATTERMOST_URL` ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà `channels.mattermost.enabled` ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô `false`)

21. ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï:

- 22. `oncall` (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô): ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å @mention
- `onmessage`: ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
- 23. `onchar`: ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå (`channels.mattermost.oncharPrefixes`, ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô `[">", "!"]`)

24. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á:

- 25. DM ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `channels.mattermost.dmPolicy="pairing"` (‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà)
- DMs ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏ò‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏∞: `channels.mattermost.dmPolicy="open"` ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö `channels.mattermost.allowFrom=["*"]`
- 26. ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°: `channels.mattermost.groupPolicy="allowlist"` ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á) 27. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `channels.mattermost.groupAllowFrom` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á

28. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `channels.mattermost.accounts` (‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô multi-account ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô) 29. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
29. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `channel:<id>` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `user:<id>` (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ `@username`) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á; id ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô id ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏•

### 31. `channels.signal` (signal-cli)

32. ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Signal ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô):

```json5
33. {
  channels: {
    signal: {
      reactionNotifications: "own", // off | own | all | allowlist
      reactionAllowlist: ["+15551234567", "uuid:123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000"],
      historyLimit: 50, // include last N group messages as context (0 disables)
    },
  },
}
```

34. ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô:

- `off`: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô
- `own`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)
- `all`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
- 35. `allowlist`: ‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å `channels.signal.reactionAllowlist` ‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô)

### 36. `channels.imessage` (imsg CLI)

37. OpenClaw ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™ `imsg rpc` (JSON-RPC ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô stdio) 38. ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï

```json5
39. {
  channels: {
    imessage: {
      enabled: true,
      cliPath: "imsg",
      dbPath: "~/Library/Messages/chat.db",
      remoteHost: "user@gateway-host", // SCP for remote attachments when using SSH wrapper
      dmPolicy: "pairing", // pairing | allowlist | open | disabled
      allowFrom: ["+15555550123", "user@example.com", "chat_id:123"],
      historyLimit: 50, // include last N group messages as context (0 disables)
      includeAttachments: false,
      mediaMaxMb: 16,
      service: "auto",
      region: "US",
    },
  },
}
```

40. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `channels.imessage.accounts` (‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô multi-account ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô)

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:

- 41. ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå Full Disk Access ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• Messages
- 42. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Messages
- 43. ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö `chat_id:<id>` 44. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `imsg chats --limit 20` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ä‡∏ï
- 45. `channels.imessage.cliPath` ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏õ‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏´‡πà‡∏≠ (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `ssh` ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á Mac ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô `imsg rpc`); ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ SSH keys ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô
- 46. ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏´‡πà‡∏≠ SSH ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏Å‡∏• ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ `channels.imessage.remoteHost` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô SCP ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `includeAttachments`

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á wrapper:

```bash
#!/usr/bin/env bash
exec ssh -T gateway-host imsg "$@"
```

### `agents.defaults.workspace`

47. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ **‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß** ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå

‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `~/.openclaw/workspace`.

```json5
{
  agents: { defaults: { workspace: "~/.openclaw/workspace" } },
}
```

48. ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô `agents.defaults.sandbox` ‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏™‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏õ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ï‡πâ `agents.defaults.sandbox.workspaceRoot`

### 49. `agents.defaults.repoRoot`

50. ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î Runtime ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á system prompt 1. ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ OpenClaw
    ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ `.git` ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏•‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã (‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô) 2. ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏ò‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

```json5
3. {
  agents: { defaults: { repoRoot: "~/Projects/openclaw" } },
}
```

### 4. `agents.defaults.skipBootstrap`

5. ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ (`AGENTS.md`, `SOUL.md`, `TOOLS.md`, `IDENTITY.md`, `USER.md`, `HEARTBEAT.md` ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ `BOOTSTRAP.md`)

6. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏•‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ ‡∏ã‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏µ‡πÇ‡∏õ

```json5
7. {
  agents: { defaults: { skipBootstrap: true } },
}
```

### 8. `agents.defaults.bootstrapMaxChars`

9. ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏Å‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ã‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏â‡∏µ‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏ô system prompt
   ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `20000`.

10. ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏â‡∏µ‡∏î‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß/‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ

```json5
11. {
  agents: { defaults: { bootstrapMaxChars: 20000 } },
}
```

### `agents.defaults.userTimezone`

12. ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö **‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á system prompt** (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πå‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏°‡∏õ‡πå‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ã‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°) 13. ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ OpenClaw ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Æ‡∏™‡∏ï‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πå

```json5
{
  agents: { defaults: { userTimezone: "America/Chicago" } },
}
```

### 14. `agents.defaults.timeFormat`

15. ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏° **‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤** ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô Current Date & Time ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á system prompt
16. ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô: `auto` (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£)

```json5
17. {
  agents: { defaults: { timeFormat: "auto" } }, // auto | 12 | 24
}
```

### `messages`
